solid #000000">&nbsp;</P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman">A few weeks ago, we announced that a Program Management Office (PMO) 
organization had been established to oversee the joint integration planning 
activities
required to position TechnipFMC for &#145;day one&#146; success and beyond. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman">Since then, our two companies have been working together to develop 
the PMO
structure, governance and operating principles, and to identify key 
appointments. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt;
font-family:Times New Roman">Overall leadership of the PMO is with Thierry 
Pilenko, Technip&#146;s
Chairman and CEO, and Doug Pferdehirt, FMC Technologies&#146; President and COO.
</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-
family:Times New Roman"><B>Executive Sponsor Team (EST) </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman">Reporting to them is the EST, which is made up of the recently 
announced leadership team of TechnipFMC.</P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman"><B>PMO Core Team </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-
bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">This team will oversee 
execution of the
pre-merger integration planning activities: </P> <P STYLE="font-
size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman"><B>Functional and Business Workstreams </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman">To date, we have established several workstreams and the majority of 
the lead appointments have been confirmed. Each workstream has at least one 
executive
sponsor. One of the key roles of the workstream leads is to ensure that the 
business and/or function and/or regional heads in the respective FMC 
Technologies and Technip organizations are fully involved in the integration 
planning process: </P>
<P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

focused on execution and serving our customers. Thank you for your continued 
support and flexibility throughout this critical pre-merger phase. </P>

cause actual results to differ materially from our historical experience and our
present expectations or projections. You should carefully consider the foregoing
factors and the other risks and uncertainties that affect the parties&#146;

including those described in FMC Technologies&#146; (&#147;FMC

with the United States Securities and Exchange Commission (the &#147;SEC&#148;)

registration documents and other documents filed from time to time with the

looking statements are often identified by the words &#147;believe,&#148;

new clients

proceedings; and the parties&#146; international operations, which are subject

SEC by Technip).

at www.technip.com. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-
